      <p class="font-12 text-white-color">
       扫码了解更多资讯
      </p>
     </div>

     <img src="/static/kejian2020/img/close-icon.png"/>
    </a>
   </div>

 </body>
 <script src="/static/kejian2020/js/jquery-3.4.1.min.js" type="text/javascript">
 </script>
 <script src="/static/kejian2020/js/layer.js" type="text/javascript">
 </script>
 <script src="/static/kejian2020/js/function.js" type="text/javascript">
 </script>
 <script src="/static/kejian2020/js/swiper.min.js" type="text/javascript">
 </script>
 <script type="text/javascript">
  $(document).ready(function () { //所有dom都准备好在执行代码

        //顶部广告动效
        // console.log($(window).scrollTop());
        setTimeout(function () {
            $('#transitionAd .top-ad-img').fadeIn('200');
        }, 100);
        //头部个人中心显示与隐藏
        $('#showUserCenter').hover(function () {
            $('#topUserCenter').show();
            this.classList.add('bg-white-color');
            $('#userTitle').addClass('text-orange-color');
            $('#userTitle').removeClass('text-white-color');
        }, function () {
            $('#topUserCenter').hide();
            this.classList.remove('bg-white-color');
            $('#userTitle').removeClass('text-orange-color');
            $('#userTitle').addClass('text-white-color');
        });
        //头部导航显示与隐藏
        $('#showTopNavigator').hover(function () {
            $('#topNavigator').show();
            this.classList.add('bg-white-color');
            $('#topNavTitle').addClass('text-orange-color');
            $('#topNavTitle').removeClass('text-white-color');
        }, function () {
            $('#topNavigator').hide();
            this.classList.remove('bg-white-color');
            $('#topNavTitle').removeClass('text-orange-color');
            $('#topNavTitle').addClass('text-white-color');
        });
        //二维码扫码轮循
        // 初始化扫描登录微信二维码
        var scan = new scanWechat();
        scan.getWechatCode('scanWechat', 120, 120);
        var scanTimer;//定义定时器
        clearInterval(scanTimer);//清空定时器，以免打开多个定时器

        //二维码登录
        $('#switchLogin').click(function () {
            if (this.src.indexOf('ewm-login') > 0) {
                this.src = '/static/kejian2020/img/pc-login.png';
                $('#pcLogin').hide();
                $('#ewmLogin').show();
                clearInterval(scanTimer);//清空定时器，以免打开多个定时器
                scanTimer = setInterval(function () {
                    scan.checkLogin('#scanWechat', scanTimer)
                }, 2000);
            } else {
                clearInterval(scanTimer);
                this.src = '/static/kejian2020/img/ewm-login.png';
                $('#pcLogin').show();
                $('#ewmLogin').hide();
            }
        });
        // 搜索框标签选择
        $('#showSearchTitle').hover(function () {
            $('#searchTitleList').show();
        }, function () {
            $('#searchTitleList').hide();
        });
        $('#searchTitleList li').click(function () {
            $('#searchTitle').html(this.innerHTML);
        });
        //更多搜索
        $('#moreSearch').hover(function () {
            $('#moreSearchList').show();
        }, function () {
            $('#moreSearchList').hide();
        });
        // 显示子类navigator
        $('#showNavContent .show-nav').hover(function () {
            this.classList.add('bg-blue-color');
            this.querySelector('.show-nav-a').classList.add('text-white-color');
            $(this.querySelector('.nav-content')).show();
        }, function () {
            this.classList.remove('bg-blue-color');
            this.querySelector('.show-nav-a').classList.remove('text-white-color');
            $(this.querySelector('.nav-content')).hide();
        });
        //焦点图swiper
        var mySwiper = new Swiper('.swiper-container', {
            loop: true, // 循环模式选项

            // 如果需要分页器
            pagination: {
                el: '.swiper-pagination',
            },

            // 如果需要前进后退按钮
            navigation: {
                nextEl: '.swiper-button-next',
                prevEl: '.swiper-button-prev',
            },
            autoplay: {
                delay: 3000
            }
        });
        //最新更新tab
        var zxgxTab = new lsTab();
        $('#newList li').click(function () {
            jpzyTab.tab('bg-white-color border-bottom-throw-2', 'text-black-l-color', '#newList li', '.new', this);
        });
        //精品资源tab
        var jpzyTab = new lsTab();
        $('#resourceList li').click(function () {
            jpzyTab.tab('bg-white-color border-bottom-throw-3', 'text-black-l-color', '#resourceList li', '.resource', this);
        });
        //题库组卷tab
        var tkzjTab = new lsTab();
        $('#questionList li').click(function () {
            tkzjTab.tab('bg-white-color border-bottom-throw-2', 'text-black-l-color', '#questionList li', '.question', this);
        });
        //教育频道tab
        var jypdTab = new lsTab();
        $('#educationList li').click(function () {
            jypdTab.tab('bg-white-color border-bottom-throw-2', 'text-black-l-color', '#educationList li', '.education', this);
        });
        //ppt资源
        var pptTab = new lsTab();
        $('#pptList li').click(function () {
            pptTab.tab('bg-white-color border-bottom-throw-3', 'text-black-l-color', '#pptList li', '.ppt', this);
        });
        //文秘公文
        var wmgwTab = new lsTab();
        $('#announceList li').click(function () {
            wmgwTab.tab('bg-white-color border-bottom-throw-3', 'text-black-l-color', '#announceList li', '.announce', this);
        });

        var showFunction = new fixedNavAndTop();
        //显示微信二维码
        showFunction.showEwm('#showQrcode', '#wxQrcode');
        //返回顶部
        showFunction.goTop('#toTop');
        //显示fixedNav
        // showFunction.showFixedNav('#fixedNav', '#closeFixedNav');

        //子nav tab
        var childTab = new lsTab(true);
        $('.childNavList li').click(function () {
            childTab.tab('text-orange-color before-orange-border', 'text-black-l-color', '.childNavList li', '.child-nav', this, $(this).parent().parent().parent());
        });

        //提取列表展现
        $('#withDraw li').hover(function () {
            $('#withDraw li .simple').each(function (index, item) {
                $(item).show();
            });
            $('#withDraw li .hard').each(function (index, item) {
                $(item).hide();
            });
            $(this).find('.hard').show();
            $(this).find('.simple').hide();
        });
        //关闭底部固定
        $('#footClosed').click(function () {
            $('#fixedFoot').hide();
            localStorage.setItem("BAD_TM",Math.round(new Date() / 1000)+86400);
        });
        var BAD_TM=localStorage.getItem("BAD_TM")
        if(BAD_TM && BAD_TM>Math.round(new Date() / 1000))
        {
            $('#fixedFoot').hide();
        }
        // 签到页面
        $('#signIn').click(function () {
            var _this = this;
            var ii = layer.load(2);
            var time_str = (Math.round(new Date() / 1000)).toString();
            var signIn = new doPost('//www.5ykj.com/member/sign.html', '');
            signIn.proFunction.then(
                function (data) {
                    console.log(data);
                    layer.msg('恭喜您！签到成功！', {icon: 1, time: 1000});
                    setLocalStorage('lastSign', time_str);
                    layer.close(ii);
                    $(_this).addClass('pointer-none');
                    $(_this).html('已签到');
                }
            );
            signIn.proFunction.catch(function (reason) {
                console.log(reason);
                layer.alert(reason);
                layer.close(ii);
            });
        });
        // 退出页面
        logOut(".log_out", window.location.href);

        tcLogin('.tc-login');

        //搜索框360站内搜索
        $("#search_button").click(
            function () {
                var keyword = $("#search_keyword").val();
                if (keyword == "") {
                    layer.msg("请输入关键字", {icon: 2, time: 2000});
                    return;
                }
                window.open("https://www.so.com/s?fr=none&rg=1&site=5ykj.com&q=" + keyword);
            }
        );
    });
 </script>
</html>
